 to bhai lagata to yahi he ki car apane liye achche khaase graahak dhund legi
 But, if you want to find the difference between this car and the rest of the SUV, then we tell you
 1
 The Ertiga built on the Swift platform has a length of 4265 millimeters, and the Innova has a length of 4585 millimeters, which means the Innova is 320 mm long
 2
 The Ertiga has a width of 1695 millimeters, and the Innova has a width of 1770 millimeters, which means the Innova is 5 millimeters wide
 3
 Its height is 1685 millimeters while the height of Innova is 1755 millimeters, ie Innova is 70 millimeters higher
 yani saaf-saaf najar aa rahaa he ki oonchai, lambaai or chaudaai main inova aage nikalati hui najar aa rahi he
 4
 yahi haal ingine kaa bhi he
 The Ertiga engine is a 1400 cc petrol engine that gives power of 95 bhp
 1300 sisi kaa dijal ingine he jo 90 biechpi kii power detaa he
 But the engine of Innova is 2000 cc in petrol which gives power of 132 bhp
 jabaki dijal me 2500 sisi kaa he jo 102 biechpi kii power detaa he

 People have many doubts about online shopping
 ye ashankaayen online frod ko lekar hoti hai or honi bhi chahie, aajkal online frod ke maamalon main jabardast oochaal jo aayaa he
 Anyway, you are not directly aware of the person who is buying the product by relying on website or website
 uski ek virtual pahchaan he, jisase aap waakif hai
 In such a situation you would think that 'cache on delivery' is a better option
 lekin 'cash on delivery' ke maamle main bhi aap apane kharide gaye product ko dekhe bina hi uski keemat chukaate hai
 That is, you pay money after seeing his panking
 aise main aap online shopping main kaise apane risk ko kam se kam kar sakate hai or kaise is tarah ke frod se batch sakate hai
 Know some solutions here 
 
 1
 Buy goods from official sellers: E-commerce websites like Amazon and Flipkart provide market places to sellers all over the world, these websites do not sell any products themselves
 haalanki in websites par sabhi vikreta ek saamaan nahin hote, kuch vikreta aise bhi hote hai jinhen in i-commers websites kaa lagbhag 'aadhikarik vikreta' mana ja saktaa he
 In the case of Flipkart, 'WS Retail' enjoys this status
 yani flipcart par is vikreta se kharidari karnaa 100 fisadi surakshit he
 Although prices may be slightly higher at 'WS Retail' than other sellers on the same website, do not be tempted
 yahi nahin 'dablyooes retail' hi flipcart par iklauta vikreta he jo 30 din kii mani back guarantee detaa he, jabaki baaki vikreta 7 se 10 din kii ritern guarantee dete hai
 Cloudtel enjoys this status on Amazon
 jabong or mintra par zyaadaatar product aadhikarik vikritaon dwaara hi beche jate hai
 Although there are third party vendors here too, try to buy your favorite thing directly from Myntra or Jabong
 or haa aadhikarik vikreta shipping time bhi kam lete hai
 2
 aise hi product khariden jo godaam main homemejan, flipcart or snapdil jaisi i-commers websites ke apane godaam hote hai, jahaan third party vikreta kaa bhi saamaan rakhaa hota he
 If you buy the goods already in the warehouse, then their shipping is done not by the third party vendor but by the website from which you have purchased
 agar aapako jaananaa ho ki jo product aap kharid rahe hai wo godaam main maujuud he yaa nahin to bataa den ki amejan par aise products ke saath 'amejan phulfild', flipcart par 'flipcart adwantage' va snapady par 'seowship' kaa tag laga rahata he
 3
 vikreta kii reating par bhi najar dalenisse pehle ki aap apni manapsand kaa product kharidne ke liye Buy kaa batan dabaaen, vikreta kii reating jarur dekh len
 Do this especially in the case of websites like ebay and Snapdeal
 dhyaan rakhen ki aise vikritaon se hi saamaan khariden jo jinhone kam se kam 50 yaa isse zyada tranjection kiye hon or unki reating bhi 90 fisadi yaa kam se kam 4 star ho
 The higher the rating, the more you can trust the seller
 4
 Do shopping on ebay Pay with 'paisapay' Although 'cash on delivery' is considered to be quite safe, but it is not as much secure as it is thought
 khaas taur par ibe tranjection ke maamle main to bilkul bhi nahin
 On ebay, if you buy a product by paying through 'paisapay', then this website does not pay the seller until the product is in your hands and you are not satisfied with it
 product milane ke baad aapaki shikaayat milte hi ibe paise ko roak leti he or aapaki samasya ko sulajhane kii koshish karti he
 If you are not happy with the product, ebay returns your money
 lekin, bataa den ki 'cash on delivery' ke maamle main ibe aapaki madad nahin karegaa
